  <script type="text/javascript">
  function jumpTo(questionNumber)
  {
    if (!window.document.assessmentInternalNavigation)
    {
      assessment.prepareForSubmit(false);
      window.document.assessmentInternalNavigation = true;
	  internalNavigationSafetyNet.delay(assessment.safetyNetDelay);
	  assessment.savingRightNow = true;
	  document.forms[ 'saveAttemptForm' ].current_question.value = questionNumber;
	  assessment.submitAttemptForm();
	}
    // Do nothing if we're navigating already.  The user may be a bit confused but they will eventually get their next question 
    return false;
  }
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">

    var submitQuestion   = "确认问题提交。";
    var submitAssessment = "测试提交确认:单击“取消”返回到测试。单击“确定”提交测验。";

    var nextQuestion = false;
    window.document.assessmentSubmitted = false; // Used to avoid double-submitting the assessment as a whole.
    //must be settable from the popup confirm save page
    window.document.assessmentSaved = false; // Used to avoid double-submitting a single question's answer TODO: I think we can eliminate this flag and allow the double-submit based on all the other flags we have.  TODO: Change to assessment.assessmentSaved

    function confirmSubmit(msg)
    {
      if (assessment.submittingRightNow)
   	  {
    	return false;
 	  }

      /* Note - the submittingRightNow flag is explicitly separate from the savingRightNow flag so that we can handle the
       * user hitting 'saveandsubmit' both while an asynchronous save is happening and while one is pending.  The savingRightNow
       * flag saves us from a conflict with an async save and the submittingRightNow flag stops new async saves from occurring.
       * Without this flag, if you answer your questions, hit saveandsubmit and then wait there for a while (10-30 seconds:
       * long enough so that a background async save could have been kicked off) and then hit 'ok' - at that point in time both
       * the background and foreground processes will submit concurrently.  By blocking the async
       * saves while we're waiting for the user to click 'ok' we avoid this concurrent submit.
       */
      assessment.submittingRightNow = true;
      assessment.savingRightNow = true;
      assessment.backtrackProhibited = false;
      try
      {
        assessment.prepareForSubmit(false);
        var validForm = validateForm();
	      // only show the "are you sure?" message if the validation succeeded
	      if ( validForm && (assessment.userReallyWantsToSubmit || window.confirm(msg) ))
	      {
	         if ( assessment.checkAlreadySubmitted(page.bundle.getString('take.dupe_warn')))
	         {
	         	
	         	 window.top.document.title = "Blackboard Learn";
	             document.forms.saveAttemptForm.method.value = 'notajax'; // Make sure we don't go through the ajax-save logic on the server - aside from that we don't care about the method value
	          	 return true; // The caller will submit the form after this.
	       	 }
	      }
      }
      catch (err)
      {
    	  // Ignore the error - just want to make sure we fall through the code below
      }

      // If we get here then either the form isn't valid to submit or the user chose not to submit
      assessment.submittingRightNow = false;
      assessment.savingRightNow = false;
      return false;
    }

    function navigate(direction) {
      if (!window.document.assessmentInternalNavigation)
      {
        // Set textarea value to VTBE contents:
        window.document.assessmentInternalNavigation = true;
        try
        {
            assessment.prepareForSubmit(false);

	        var validForm = true;
	        
	        if ( validForm)
	        {
	          assessment.savingRightNow = true;
	          internalNavigationSafetyNet.delay(assessment.safetyNetDelay);
	          document.forms.saveAttemptForm.method.value = 'notajax'; // Make sure we don't go through the ajax-save logic on the server - aside from that we don't care about the method value
              document.forms.saveAttemptForm.navigationTarget.value=direction;
	          try
	          {
	            assessment.submitAttemptForm();
	          }
	          catch (err)
	          {
	            // so we can clear this in error cases:
	          }
              document.forms.saveAttemptForm.navigationTarget.value='';
	        }
	        else
	        {
	          window.document.assessmentInternalNavigation = false;
	        }
        }
        catch (err)
        {
        	window.document.assessmentInternalNavigation = false;
        }
      }
      return false;
    }


  if (window.addEventListener)
    window.addEventListener("load", staticbar, false);
  else if (window.attachEvent)
   window.attachEvent("onload", staticbar);
  else if (document.getElementById)
    window.onload=staticbar;
  </script>

  }
  );

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var course_id = "_1287_1";
   var courseTitle = "毛泽东思想和中国特色社会主义理论体系概论2015（张良）";
